<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2f9a9535-5314-4e76-9b1a-bf3a918e0f7e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer1129415076649891879"><b>Re-read: 22.10.14</b><br/><b>Third re-read: 26.04.15.</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"To find the goal, you must concentrate, for within these walls there is one at stake. Which path would you prefer to take? Death, or life, the choice is yours, but keep in mind, even immortals can make mistakes."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>*Might contain spoilers*</b><br/>Holy shit, this book was perfect! Seriously, it couldn't be more perfect, if you asked me. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392584891ra/8580844.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Take the path for which you seek, but keep in mind, not all will take you to what you need. Illusions abound, </i></b></blockquote></span>

  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>*Might contain spoilers*</b><br>Holy shit, this book was perfect! Seriously, it couldn't be more perfect, if you asked me. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392584891ra/8580844.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Take the path for which you seek, but keep in mind, not all will take you to what you need. Illusions abound, tempt and deceive, and while men covet that which holds great beauty, humility is often the kay to the King's needs."</i>

  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And Ryder... Possessive, protective, powerful, sexy, dominant.. Ahh man, i want him! He's a man who loves control, and is so freaking powerful that he can pretty much kill anyone he likes.. Ryder's a beast, but fuck, he's one hell of a hot beast! He's perfect, and the best leader anyone could have. Ryder will pretty much sacrifice everything for his people, for his land, no matter of his own wants. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392584891ra/8580846.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You've got a great ass," he said, never taking his eyes from mine as we walked, oblivious to anyone watching us. "Your screams when i fuck you? I like that shit, too. The noises you make when i drive my cock balls deep and you ask for more? Fuck, i seriously like it… a lot."</i>

</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Goddammit, Pet, See me!" He shouted as the walls shook around us.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Aodan, if you want to keep your hands, i suggest you get them off of her," Ryder growled as he reached for me and pulled me against his body.<br>"Just seeing if she's into me, my King."<br>"She's not," Ristan said..</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Syn... So beautiful, fierce, kind and strong! I want to be her, for real! I'm jealous of how she handles things and how she fights for what she wants.. More secrets keeps coming her way, and more struggle and lies keeps pushing her down, but does she stay down? Hell no! Syn's a fighter, a real warrior who still doesn't take shit from anyone, not even Ryder. In 'Escaping Destiny' you actually got to know Syn in a whole new way. She's vulnerable and she's got her hormones running all over the place, and she has no idea how to cope with eveything that is going on. I love how, when she feels down, Syn still fight. Amelia Hutchins wrote so fantastic that even though Syn struggled hard and was scared, she didn't seem weak at all. For me, it actually made Syn even stronger. I seriously admire her!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392584891ra/8580847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Anyone ever consider the idea that maybe Danu ate a batch of funky brownies and decided to send Ristan some very random, very kinky dreams? Or, maybe Ristan ate the brownies? It's plausible with that Demon."</i>

</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Me and bombs are on a first name basis," was my reply, which cause her to look at me as if i was insane. "We are close, like this," i crossed my fingers and wiggled my eyebrow, trying to reassure her i was fine.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The passion, and the want between Ryder and Syn is so powerful that i almost exploded! I have to admit that i don't think i have ever shipped a couple more than those two.. They had me crying, while screaming in anger and it could suddenly shift from anger to freaking love... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392589659ra/8581231.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If you keep smiling with that damn grin on your lips, I'm going to fuck you."<br>"That's a bad thing, how?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Princess," he smiled wider.<br>"Fairy," I groanded.<br>(…..)<br>"Witch," he amended.<br>"Asshat," I growled and narrowed my eyes.<br>"Okay!" Ristan clapped loud enough that we both turned our glares on him. "Now that we got the foreplay out of the way, we can get right onto the main course."<br>Ryder snorted, and i crossed my arms.<br>"Ryder," Ristan said patiently, and i could tell they were doing the mind thing again from the look passing over their faces.<br>"I'm trying. She's the one who started it!"</i>

</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>

It was tempting, but at the same time, i wanted him to trust me. <br>"You carry my child inside of you," his hand moved to touch my stomach. "There is no fucking chance of anything happening to either of you. Even if that means that i have to protect you from yourself."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You sound jealous," he purred.<br>"Suck it, Fairy!"<br>"I don't plan to suck anything. I plan to lick it until it flows down my face. Now answer the question; are you jealous?" he continued.<br>(…..) "And if i was?"<br>"Are you?"<br>"If i was?"<br>"Are you?"<br>"Are we, what?" Ristan asked…</i>

</blockquote><br><blockquote>__________________</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Lay with me, Pet. I'm in need of you."</i>

If Syn wasn't with Ryder, then, damn, i have to admit that i would then ship Ristan and Syn.. But i do ship their friendship! Ristan's relationship with Ryder is perfect! He isn't afraid to tell what is on his mind, even if it pisses Ryder off. He's pretty much the best friend anyone want to have..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385272352ra/7114408.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I like my head on my shoulders. If you so much as get a scratch on your delicate flesh, Ryder will remove it!"</i>
</b><br><br>I couldn't stop reading once i started on it, and damn, Escaping Destiny just became my favorite book of 2014, perhaps even favorite book of all time! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392584891ra/8580848.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book had literally everything a book should have, and more! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392589659ra/8581232.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Amelia Hutchins is a brilliant author, who deserves tons of awards for this series! </b><br><br><br>Book three of this series was full of Action, Lusty sex, and Murder. This is a fast paced, ball of angst. Ryder loves Synthia. He is just in denial that his whole world revolves around her. I can't get enough of these two and the Freaky Sexual Horde King. I can't wait to see how this all will end in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1341925269" rel="nofollow noopener">Seducing Destiny</a><br><br><br><br><b>My Fae Chronicles reviews:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/872766086" rel="nofollow noopener">Fighting Destiny</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1317628930" rel="nofollow noopener">Taunting Destiny</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1331229894" rel="nofollow noopener">Escaping Destiny</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1341925269" rel="nofollow noopener">Seducing Destiny</a></b></span>

She is trapped no way out and worried that Ryder will get himself killed trying to save her from the Horde King. Things are looking really bad for Syn!<br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/shocked_happy_zpsgyirx6e6.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Holy Plot twist batman!!! <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Ryder is the Mother Fuckin Horde King!!!!! <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I so didn't see that shit coming! It's 5% into the damn book and I am floored! An</span>
  <span id="freeText13024836027246745292" style="display:none"><b>5 Wee Little Beasties Stars</b><br><br><b> *Spoilers*</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/MyGodThatsAmazing_zpsu8en0p1l.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>This book was Amazing!!!! So the book starts right were Taunting Destiny left off Syn is being gifted to the Horde King. She is trapped no way out and worried that Ryder will get himself killed trying to save her from the Horde King. Things are looking really bad for Syn!<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/shocked_happy_zpsgyirx6e6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

It's 5% into the damn book and I am floored! And the plot twist just kept coming. <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Ryder%20book%203_zpsswekew9z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Ryder OMG I think I just fell in love with Ryder. He was so damn sexy, protective, powerful as fuck ,dominant , and Possessive, Damn if he didn't really try in this book to make Syn happy and be romantic. He is trying to see where she is coming from and is starting to give a little instead of always taking! Ryder really grows in this book, and nothing is sexier than a tough man falling hard for a woman. OH and he is one Panty melting , dirty talking beast!<br><br><b>"It may be between your legs, Pet, but make no mistake, this belongs to me. Understand?"<br><br>"Good girls get special kisses. Do you want to be kissed?"<br><br><br>"I'm going to fuck you so hard, and so deep that you will scream my name, Princess. Your body will tremble, your insides will melt, you will be wild with need, but you won't come, not until i allow it. I want you so fucking wild with lust that you beg me to come. That you will beg me to allow you to find release, and only then will i allow you to come on my tongue."</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_m1o8gv12yS1qhccgw_zps0akpuib8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Syn came out swinging in this book. I didn't think she could get any better for me, but I was wrong.<br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/syn%20book%203_zpsq7syz95s.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Syn has always been Kick ass, but in this book she shows a softer and vulnerable side. She really fights for want she wants !<br><br><br><b>"You want me fine? Leave me alone for a minute. In the last few weeks I have watched my best friend be murdered right in front of me, I found out I wasn't human, I have been stabbed by Zahruk, almost blown up, given to the Dark Heir as his fiancee, Kidnapped, met my fairy fucking family, and now I'm a whore for the fucking Horde King! You want me to be okay? Then get the fuck back for five minutes!"<br><br>"I'm going to fight for him. He's my ever after, Adam. I'm willing to fight to keep him,"<br><br>"It fucking hurts! I can't breathe, Ryder, because of you! Before you I was fine. I was living. I could breathe and without you I can't! When Adrian died it hurt like hell, but I could breathe, damn it!"</b><br><br>God did I hurt with them. My emotions wow this book had me feeling everything. I loved Ryder and Syn's relationship in this book they are a lot more like a couple and you can see their love growing . They had a very cute playfulness in this book that I loved.<br><br><b><br>“She’s my fucking anchor, and no one will take her from me again, not even to save this world.”<br><br><br>“I was going to fight to keep the elusive Horde King as my own. Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.” </b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/ryderand%20syn%20book%203_zpshjajilwv.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422742885ra/13540916.gif" alt=" photo ryderand syn book 3_zpshjajilwv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For real I am loving me some Ristan! This book consumed me from beginning to end, kept me on edge , was action and drama packed. Damn good read!! <br><br>Fav quote:<br>“I'm the fucking Horde King, I don't woo."<br>"Woo her," Ristan continues.<br>"I don't woo."<br>"Woo," he repeats.<br>"I'm not the kind of man to woo anyone. I can make her scream my name to the rafters, isn't that enough wooing?"<br>"Woo," Ristan smirks, which only served to irritate me more.<br>"Woo," I grind out on an exhale.<br>"Yes, woo," he says, already turning to walk away. I watch his shoulders quake with laughter.<br>"Woo," I growl.<br>"Woo!" He says over his shaking shoulders.<br>"Fuck me," I shake my head.<br>"No thanks, not my type...” <br><br>GOD I can't freaking wait for SD!!!!! If you have not read this series you should totally check it out!<br><br><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer842961953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15631137717965866471"><b>
  <i>4 Look Inside The Beast Stars!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394353883i/8841823.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.</i>
</b> <br/><br/>The 3rd installment in The Fae Chronicles, was hot, action packed and chocka-blocked full of my favourite fairy Ryder! After the mother of all cliffys at the end of Taunting Destiny I was in a state of near panic! The first couple of pages into Escaping Destiny and I was swearing like a sailor and just about to start balling like a baby!!! This was quite possibly the best intro I have ever read!<br/><br/>A lot of issues </span>
  <span id="freeText15631137717965866471" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>4 Look Inside The Beast Stars!!!</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394353883i/8841823.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.</i>
</b> <br><br>The 3rd installment in The Fae Chronicles, was hot, action packed and chocka-blocked full of my favourite fairy Ryder! After the mother of all cliffys at the end of Taunting Destiny I was in a state of near panic! The first couple of pages into Escaping Destiny and I was swearing like a sailor and just about to start balling like a baby!!! This was quite possibly the best intro I have ever read!<br><br>A lot of issues are cleared up in Escaping Destiny, which is why I feel like it's one of those necessary books. It was quite enjoyable but to be honest it paled in comparison to the first two books. Our characters Syn and Ryder are multi-faceted and we see one of those sides. Syn is still strong, obstinate and her personality compliments Ryder perfectly.<br><br>We're shown a different side of Ryder, have no fear he's still the original alpha male, but he's also caring, willing to compromise to be able to keep the woman he loves in his life. This was awesome but I do prefer douche nugget Ryder.<br><br>The children of faerie are dying, and Syn is part of the key to their salvation. There is also a powerful enemy that is hell bent on destroying faerie and it's people. We're given an incredible amount of information in this book, but again it was necessary.<br><br>Ryder and Syn's relationship blossomed and matured in this book, and seeing that this is PNR, I felt that it was surprisingly realistic. I have very high hopes for the next book, Seducing Destiny. Amelia Hutchins has a way with words, she grabs the readers attention doesn't let go till the end, and even then she leaves you wanting more!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393092317ra/8660744.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=tales-of-the-sexy-weres">tales-of-the-sexy-weres</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer789492194" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11155693840391069558">Whoa... This novel surprised me, and as you can see by the score, not in a good way. <br/><br/>I have waited for this book like an alchie for happy hour. Wanted, no needed the next Hutchins novel! In just a few books this woman gave me whiplash with her plot twists, made me grind my teeth with the action and burned my retinas with her sensuality. She got an insta-fan! <br/><br/>Prior to this we left off with Syn being at the clutches of the Horde King the meanest, baddest guy around. I know, right???? And now we ha</span>
  <span id="freeText11155693840391069558" style="display:none">Whoa... This novel surprised me, and as you can see by the score, not in a good way. <br /><br />I have waited for this book like an alchie for happy hour. Wanted, no needed the next Hutchins novel! In just a few books this woman gave me whiplash with her plot twists, made me grind my teeth with the action and burned my retinas with her sensuality. She got an insta-fan! <br /><br />Prior to this we left off with Syn being at the clutches of the Horde King the meanest, baddest guy around. I know, right???? And now we have Escaping Destiny. What does a hurricane say to the palm tree??? Hold on to your nuts, this isn't a regular blow job!!!! And if the previous books are anything to go by this one will be a spectacular ride in the world of the Fae. Right? <br /><br />Sorry to say but wrong.....<br /><br />I have expected so much more from the Horde. I mean....it's 'THE HORDE'! The Fae are stuff of nightmares for the humans, The Horde are stuff of nightmares for the Fae. I have expected fountains of blood, dark and dangerous enchanted castles, great halls filled with chilling monstrosities and with the Fae using sex to feed, the possibilities were endless.<br /><br />Instead I got landed smack in the middle of an Lisa friggin' Kleypas novel. The main focus of this story was Syn trying to carve out her piece of heaven between all the concubines in the Horde King's harem. Not much more happened. Gone was the ass-kicking, take-no-shit, itchy Witchy and instead welcome the swoony, pining, angsty heroine in a full skirt. How in the fuck that happened? <br /><br />From the previous novels we know how manipulative the Fae could be. By Hutchins' own words it's the Fae way. Did the women do something sneaky and clever to trap Syn??? Nop. They were whiney and openly bitchy. So no fun there, no conflicts and no action.<br /><br />We are in the Fairie, how about spells and magic??? In the previous novels we had mind reading, manipulation, wards, poisoning, and all sorts of shenanigans. In this novel the magic is used to conjure nighties and up-does, sometimes even furniture. :( ??!!!<br /><br />How about Ryder's men? That are protective, loyal and to the point, and will do everything to help heal the Fairie? They were honest with Syn before and held back no punches. Now they slowly became the leaders of the 'Cheer for Syn' parade. <br /><br />And Ryder? He said so many times before. I am Fae, not human, I am the baddest motherfucker out there. In this novel, i didn't see it. He was pressed against the wall,stressed out and unable to deal with half the shit that came his way. In the end he wound up changing some of the ancient rules of the Fairie that he swore to protect. Big hit and miss there. After that he wasn't as Fae in my eyes as before, he was so much more human. Sadly. He lost all the otherworldly attributes of Ryder the fucking Fairy. <br /><br />In the very beginning the lid is blown by Ryder coming clean to Syn. The end result is simple- there is no more mystery. We now know absolutely everything. There could have been many options to execute this story- switching between the Horde King and Ryder, keeping us on our toes. Is he??? Isn't he???? And a blank canvass for all the emotions that Syn might feel loving Ryder, and being attracted to the Horde King. <br /><br />The great Goddess Danu was a character that was introduced solely for the info-dumps. Every time she shows up she winds up explaining herself and everything she does. There wasn't a feel of godliness about her, or agelessness. She was supposed to be the terrifying spirit of the Fairie, but read like a fairy godmother. <br /><br />It simply lacked everything. I found myself constantly waiting for things to happen. Even the labyrinth tests were simple and predictable. There was one big fight scene at the end of it all that kinda kept it all afloat, but blew up in my face with Syn becoming half goddess uber-Fae. Everything seemed like it was handed to her on a platter and she didn't fight for anything. I wouldn't have waited for Ryder to change the laws about the marriage. Syn's higher up then Ryder's fiancee, right? The old ass-kicker would spend some of the time in the library looking for a way out and dunno, have a duel or something. She was a killer before, and now a deadly Fae, to combine those two things we should have been set for a fallout of massive proportions. Again by Hutchins' own words the Fae fight for what they want by proving they are the better mate. It would have been so much better if Syn got off her ass and did something about it herself. One more thing that seriously grated on my nerves was the fact that all her inability to do anything to help herself was placed down to her being hormonal....from the pregnancy...*grinds teeth* <br /><br />I was just disappointed by the end of it all. It seemed so rushed and not at all a Hutchins novel. I understand the hardship that she must be feeling these days and the pressure from the fans. I mean she knew she had a winner on her hands with the very first novel, and her popularity just exploded leaving her to deal with a mass of 'Gimme-Gimmes' (myself included), but personally if i had to wait another 5 months to get the next book i would have, gladly, if the end result was different. The only reason for just a two star mark is this: Hutchins herself set a helluva high standard, and from her work we all know that she is more then capable of delivering. This novel however skated on the lines of cliche-hood the entire time. She is a brilliant new writer that has a chance of being one of the most popular writers of the genre out there. But this was not up to standards that she set. Still i am in her corner every step of the way and looking forward to the next one. There is so much talent in this woman, can't wait to see what happens next, and hope for the best.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11155693840391069558" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1273030406" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1273030406" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1273030406?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1273030406" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14660547327097379386"><br/><b>
  <i>Bitches love big libraries.</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/true%20dat' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>In our last episode, we found out that Synthia was being given to the Horde King as a gift. The Horde King is known for torturing, maiming, raping, and killing his women. But, hey, Synthia's dad had promised to give her up to him... his hands are tied. Let the torture and raping begin!<br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/get%20this%20party%20started' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/>Thanks, Dad!<br/><br/>Well, it's not a spoiler to tell you that Ryder is the Horde King. It is revealed pretty quickly. But, not quickly enough!! First, he makes sure that Synthia doesn</span>
  <span id="freeText14660547327097379386" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>Bitches love big libraries.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/true%20dat" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430893217i/14775996.png" alt="true dat photo: True Dat TrueDat.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In our last episode, we found out that Synthia was being given to the Horde King as a gift. The Horde King is known for torturing, maiming, raping, and killing his women. But, hey, Synthia's dad had promised to give her up to him... his hands are tied. Let the torture and raping begin!<br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/get%20this%20party%20started" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430893217ra/14775997.gif" alt="get this party started photo: get this party started anigif_enhanced-buzz-28705-13826433.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Thanks, Dad!<br><br>Well, it's not a spoiler to tell you that Ryder is the Horde King. It is revealed pretty quickly. But, not quickly enough!! First, he makes sure that Synthia doesn't know it is him and scares the crap out of her. He also ties her up to rape her as his alter-ego before revealing who he really is. What a great guy! If my husband/boyfriend/enemy ever pulled this shit on me, he would no longer have the equipment necessary to play this rapey game that is somehow acceptable to Synthia. <br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/kick%20in%20the%20balls" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br>That would be step one.. with the sharp stuff coming in next.<br><br>Oh, but don't worry, they are happily in love. Just one small detail, though.... Ryder is engaged to another woman, so Synthia only gets to be his concubine (that means whore, in case you didn't know). Hey, he's been betrothed since his birth, what can he do? He has to marry this other woman and have sex with her. It's his responsibility! His hands are tied. And, Synthia is such a bitch about it. Poor poor Ryder! So misunderstood. All he wants to do is marry another woman, have sex with her, keep a compound full of other concubines, and keep Synthia as his girl. Is that asking too much?? <br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/misunderstood" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430893217i/14775999.png" alt="misunderstood photo: skullpng0004.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>sleep with your eyes open, A-hole!<br><br>But, don't worry for our dear heroine because there is good news - the wonderful Horde King got her pregnant. What's worse than being a whore? Being a pregnant whore! And, these two winners are going to make great parents! Just look at what happens at their ultrasound appointment:<br><br><b>
  <i>"There's a head.. and there's another one."<br>"Oh my God, my baby has two heads," I cried.<br>"Can he live like that?" Ryder asked. </i>
</b><br><br>So, the babies will be pretty <b>and smart</b> with these genes being passed down.<br><br>Also, Ryder has assured Synthia that she will be his Number One Concubine. Isn't that special? What a guy! This is a sweet romance. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14615937635414198253"><b>
  <i>”Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>I was anxiously awaiting this third installment in <i>The Fae Chronicles</i> because the last book left me frantic to find out what would happen to Syn with The Horde King. By 11 percent, all was well in my world and I was more than happy with the direction the author brought the story. Truthfully, from this point on the excitement kinda waned for me.<br/><br/>Syn is with the Horde King, pregnant and concubined. She spends a lot of time with my favorite Demon. S</span>
  <span id="freeText14615937635414198253" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.”</i>
</b><br><br>I was anxiously awaiting this third installment in <i>The Fae Chronicles</i> because the last book left me frantic to find out what would happen to Syn with The Horde King. By 11 percent, all was well in my world and I was more than happy with the direction the author brought the story. Truthfully, from this point on the excitement kinda waned for me.<br><br>Syn is with the Horde King, pregnant and concubined. She spends a lot of time with my favorite Demon. She embarks on a quest with the group who are still trying to collect relics and she feeds a lot... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392733134ra/8602501.gif" width="375" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Syn’s true identity just keeps changes. By the end of the story, I think we have a good idea of who and what she actually is and who she will be to her love.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I don’t want to be your world; I just want to be your favorite part of it.”</i>
</b><br><br>There are some snares in Syn’s hea and the fate of Faery and this story leaves in somewhat of a cliffhanger. I’m pretty positive that this world will be saved, Syn will embrace her true self and hopefully end up with my favorite faery! <br><br><b>
  <i>”You have to trust what you are, and what you want the most, to find who you truly are.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17927559.Fighting_Destiny__The_Fae_Chronicles___1_" title="Fighting Destiny (The Fae Chronicles, #1) by Amelia Hutchins" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1460437595" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11258825764243679894"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588015142i/29366574.jpg' alt='20817046' width='318' height='243' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So Synthia is being gifted as a concubine to the Horde King as previously promised to preserve the fragile peace between the Horde and Blood kingdoms.<br/>Syn is now placing faith in Ryder to ride to her rescue as her white knight before it’s too late.<br/>But things aren’t always as they seem In Faery and Syn is In for some major shocks and reveals when her eyes are finally opened to the truth of it all and secrets are finally revealed.<br/>So this one takes place predominately in the Otherworld as Syn tries </span>
  <span id="freeText11258825764243679894" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588015142i/29366574.jpg" alt="20817046" width="318" height="243" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So Synthia is being gifted as a concubine to the Horde King as previously promised to preserve the fragile peace between the Horde and Blood kingdoms.<br>Syn is now placing faith in Ryder to ride to her rescue as her white knight before it’s too late.<br>But things aren’t always as they seem In Faery and Syn is In for some major shocks and reveals when her eyes are finally opened to the truth of it all and secrets are finally revealed.<br>So this one takes place predominately in the Otherworld as Syn tries to acclimatise to her new circumstances and condition.<br>She’s also struggling with her new reality and her place and importance in Ryder's life.<br>While Ryder himself really need to step it up before he unintentionally loses what’s most precious to him.<br>He really could take some lessons from his beast who himself knows exactly what it wants when it comes to there little pet.<br>It’s all about priority’s really and balancing the human and Fae culture and expectations that come along with it all.<br>Syn may now be fae herself but she has the heart of a human.<br>There are old and new Jealousies rising and trials to traverse and I really adored how close Syn is in this to Ristan or the Demon as she affectionately calls him.<br>He’s in a way taken on Adams responsibility’s as her closest confidant and he is ever so protective of his flower.<br>This one also seemed to have a more mystical vibe to it than its two predecessors.<br>Really enjoyed this a lot and with the war with the mages starting to take centre stage and looming on the horizon, things are really starting to intensify.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588015142i/29366573.jpg" alt="20817046" width="318" height="168" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reviewed By Beckie <div id="review_788324926" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/788324926" />
    <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger"><img alt="Zakirrah BookBlogger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396291066p2/15894726.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/788324926?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zakirrah BookBlogger" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger">Zakirrah BookBlogger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=blog-tour">blog-tour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer788324926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18416314309690722672"><b>4.5-5 Fukin Fairy Loving Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393800837i/8765468._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What can I say? Bravo Amelia Hutchins you have done it again! This is book 3 of the Fae chronicles and what a brilliant book it is. This series has me hooked.Yes, Yes I am a addict and I regret nothing!The complex characters, the storyline, the twists, the connection, hotness and much more..this book has it all! Once you start it you just can't help it, you crave more and more. So yeah each time we have to wait for the next book to be released?..yeah that is just </span>
  <span id="freeText18416314309690722672" style="display:none"><b>4.5-5 Fukin Fairy Loving Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393800837i/8765468._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say? Bravo Amelia Hutchins you have done it again! This is book 3 of the Fae chronicles and what a brilliant book it is. This series has me hooked.Yes, Yes I am a addict and I regret nothing!The complex characters, the storyline, the twists, the connection, hotness and much more..this book has it all! Once you start it you just can't help it, you crave more and more. So yeah each time we have to wait for the next book to be released?..yeah that is just torture!<br><br>If you have stumbled across this review randomly and haven't started this series..errr wtf are you waiting for?!! Get your arse into gear and dive into this series because you will not regret it!<br><br><br><i>
  <b>'Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.'</b>
</i><br><br><br>This book continues from where Book 2 left off and gets right to it.I was soo glad that this didn't drag I was scared that Ryder and Syn would be separated for too long and I would get annoyed but oohh the twist was like oh my god I thought this but then eh? omg I'm confused but pheww! haha for those of you who haven't read it probably thinking err what is this girl talking about?! Ahh you got to read it to get it ;)<br><br><br><i>
  <b>'Fate pushed us together,but destiny knew we belonged together.'</b>
</i><br><br><br>You find out in book 2 that Syn is pregnant and I was like Oh yeahh! Totally doing a happy dance coz I was just so happy that the baby was Ryder's!! And thankfully Adam and Syn didn't have to get married.All that caused me to dislike Adam but thankfully I didn't feel any anger towards him in this book and liked him as long as he isn't with Syn.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431980ra/867172.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hormonal Syn and an overprotective Ryder oh yeah this was so good!In this book Syn was in a more fragile state and things changed she isn't always the stubborn woman you met in book 1 and 2.You get to see a different side to Syn and it built her character..okay maybe I lied she is still stubborn as hell but instead of lying to herself about her feelings she learns to accept them and learns to fight for those she loves.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"Goddammit, Pet, See me!" He shouted as the walls shook around us.</b>
</i><br><br><br>You also see a different side to Ryder and we find out more about the Beast.I love the Beast ;) You see the Beast is much simpler than Ryder.He wants something, he takes it, he owns it he doesn't hold back on how he feels. Ryder is much more in-depth character who has trouble expressing his feelings at times.But in this book you see changes and both of the characters develop and grow.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393803245i/8765836._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh and before I forget Ristan is now one of my favourite characters! Yes he bloody rocks! I want a hot, hilarious Demon best friend..where can I find one? I had a soft spot for Ristan in book 1 and as the book went on I fell in love with him but in this book he became so much more.This book wouldn't be the same without him..actually this series wouldn't. He adds an element of perviness to the mix haha naww he is just brilliant I loved how he was helping Ryder and Syn with their relationship issues.And I am rooting for Danu and Ristan! You go get her boy ;)<br><br>If you are looking for a book filled with action,humour, sexiness, twists and turns leaving you craving for more this is definitely the book for you! I couldn't stop reading, yeah I read all through the night and then hated myself for reading so fast because I had finished it and now what? WHAT am I supposed to do now huh? <br><br><br><i>
  <b>"This is heaven,Synthia.Inside of you is my heaven",he whispered so softly that I wasn't even sure he had said it.</b>
</i><br><br><br>Please, Please hurry with the next book, there is only so much this addict can take! <br><br><b>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~**~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br>**ARC courtesy of the author in exchange for an honest review**<br><br>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/</a><br><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirrahs-Book-Blog/486887338054979">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr...</a><br><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18416314309690722672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833172755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6372539974511252559">It's Live!!!!<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Escaping-Destiny-Chronicles-Genevieve-Scholl-ebook/dp/B00IH487I8/ref=sr_1_4?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1392514996&sr=1-4&keywords=escaping+destiny'>http://www.amazon.com/Escaping-Destin...</a><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>4 - Fuckin Fairy! - Stars</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>AGHHHHHH!!! SQUEAL!!! </b> Synthia and Ryder!! Love them together!!! A few new developments have occurred since our last book and let me tell you I think it was written out brilliantly! I really like the direction this story is taking.<br/><br/>At the end of the last book I was scared for what was to come in this book…We left off the last book with Synthia being sent to the Horde as the payment for her brother Liam.<br/><br/> <a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_inline_mkk6e1rAPy1raaalo_zps697853f1.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/530699.gif' alt='aghhhhhh photo tumblr_inline_mkk6e1rAPy1raaalo_zps697853f1.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>But luck</span>
  <span id="freeText6372539974511252559" style="display:none">It's Live!!!!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Escaping-Destiny-Chronicles-Genevieve-Scholl-ebook/dp/B00IH487I8/ref=sr_1_4?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1392514996&amp;sr=1-4&amp;keywords=escaping+destiny">http://www.amazon.com/Escaping-Destin...</a><br><br><br><b>
  <i>4 - Fuckin Fairy! - Stars</i>
</b><br><br><b>AGHHHHHH!!! SQUEAL!!! </b> Synthia and Ryder!! Love them together!!! A few new developments have occurred since our last book and let me tell you I think it was written out brilliantly! I really like the direction this story is taking.<br><br>At the end of the last book I was scared for what was to come in this book…We left off the last book with Synthia being sent to the Horde as the payment for her brother Liam.<br><br> <a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_inline_mkk6e1rAPy1raaalo_zps697853f1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/530699.gif" alt="aghhhhhh photo tumblr_inline_mkk6e1rAPy1raaalo_zps697853f1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But luckily Ryder came through to save the day!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Goddammit, Pet, See me!" He shouted as the walls shook around us. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392666520ra/8591847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thank Goodness! I was freaking out for a minute there!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Fate pushed us together, but destiny knew we belonged together." </i>
</b><br><br>I was hoping Synthia would kick his ass for everything he put her through though.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_ma2n0nfdXZ1r3ovdbo1_250_zps55509243.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392666520ra/8591848.gif" alt="hit photo tumblr_ma2n0nfdXZ1r3ovdbo1_250_zps55509243.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Synthia is trying to learn how to fit in in the wonderful Horde Kingdom. She makes many friends, but also has a few enemies. Claire (aka super bitch!) I kept waiting for them to throw down.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/lg3CIbj_zps2d3babfb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392666520ra/8591849.gif" alt=" photo lg3CIbj_zps2d3babfb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Syn is lonely and misses of course Adam and Adrian, but is making do with what she can and Ristan is a great companion to her. I absolutely LOVE HIM!! Best Demon BFF ever!<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/2-4_zps41d5f7ce.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387467199ra/7600575.gif" alt="MMM HMMM photo 2-4_zps41d5f7ce.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So what direction do they go from here? Is everything already planned out by Danu? Do they have the free will to change things? Will they be able to save Faery themselves?<br><br><b>
  <i>"You choose which path you take to get to the end. But in the end, you are where destiny wanted you to be."</i>
</b><br><br>While Synthia and Ryder try to figure out how to save the kingdom of Faery from the evil mages, they also try to work on their relationship. Finally Synthia gets to meet Ryder’s beast in the flesh. And she gives him a run for his money.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine."</i>
</b><br><br>Beast<br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/beauty-and-the-beast-Favimcom-545082_zpsedecb1e8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392667163ra/8591905.gif" alt=" photo beauty-and-the-beast-Favimcom-545082_zpsedecb1e8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ryder<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392682058ra/8594142.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the sex with Synthia and beast mode Ryder? Hot. HOT <b>HOT!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"This is heaven, Synthia. Inside of you is my heaven."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_lm3duwJpF31qecw4to1_500_zpsee57b3ad.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392666520ra/8591850.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lm3duwJpF31qecw4to1_500_zpsee57b3ad.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Problems arise in their relationship because Ryder is under contract to marry awful Claire’s sister! What should Syn do??<br><br><b>
  <i>"I can fight for love, Demon. I just won’t compete for it. I shouldn’t have to."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_mcmq5xRYoo1ra2xd4o1_500_zps7dbc814f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392666520ra/8591851.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mcmq5xRYoo1ra2xd4o1_500_zps7dbc814f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Who from the other kingdoms will ally with them to save Faery? They need to figure it out and soon!<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/Britney-Fuck-You_zps76112fe2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392666520ra/8591852.gif" alt=" photo Britney-Fuck-You_zps76112fe2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So since I enjoyed this book what the 4 rating? Well I do feel that this was somewhat of a filler book and also I still had the problem with too much repetition of what was happening. It was still a very enjoyable read though!<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6372539974511252559" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2105052293?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2105052293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11716184551906360492"><blockquote>
  <b>“She’s my fucking anchor, and no one will take her from me again, not even to save this world.” </b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1529298435i/25811044._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Escaping Destiny</b> is the third book in The Fae Chronicles. This paranormal phenomenon continues to captivate me. I cannot seem to turn the pages fast enough! I am dying to know what will happen next! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><blockquote>
  <b>“He’s my drug of choice, and I don’t think there’s a rehab for it.”</b>
</blockquote> Syn has been swept away to live at the mercy of the Horde King. Terrified of what her future holds, she is desperate for Ryder to</span>
  <span id="freeText11716184551906360492" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>“She’s my fucking anchor, and no one will take her from me again, not even to save this world.” </b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1529298435i/25811044._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Escaping Destiny</b> is the third book in The Fae Chronicles. This paranormal phenomenon continues to captivate me. I cannot seem to turn the pages fast enough! I am dying to know what will happen next! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>“He’s my drug of choice, and I don’t think there’s a rehab for it.”</b>
</blockquote> Syn has been swept away to live at the mercy of the Horde King. Terrified of what her future holds, she is desperate for Ryder to rescue her. When the truth is revealed, she is completely dumbstruck. Ryder and Syn begin to grow and understand each other on a deeper level. In addition to the passion that has always bloomed between the two, now they learn all there is to know about each other and the crazy universe in which they live. <blockquote>
  <b>“I’m not the kind of man to woo anyone. I can make her scream my name to the rafters, isn’t that enough wooing?”</b>
</blockquote> Told in dual POV, I cannot recommend this series enough. In <b>Escaping Destiny</b>, the stakes are high for these two to come together and find a way. The dialogue flows fluidly as the tension rises for this couple. The plot is complex so it is imperative that you pay close attention to all of the characters and their relationships. If you have the opportunity, I highly recommend reading this series from the beginning back to back. With action, passion, and tender romance, this paranormal romance certainly aims to please! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, <b>Escaping Destiny</b> is an absolute must-read for Fae Chronicles fans. Syn and Ryer is one couple that has found permanent residency in my "favorite epic couple shelf". <br><br><b>***The Fae Chronicles***<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17927559.Fighting_Destiny__The_Fae_Chronicles___1_" title="Fighting Destiny (The Fae Chronicles, #1) by Amelia Hutchins" rel="nofollow noopener"><img   <span id="freeText8599973300922299665" style="display:none">Oh oh oh myyyy.... It has a COVER!!!<br><br><a href="http://s54.photobucket.com/user/robynize/media/Supernatural%20%20Folder/Supernatural%20Reaction%20Gifs/Excited/beckyexcitdjumping_zps3dd2d099.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <b>“Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.”</b>

  <b>“Every beauty needed a beast, and he was mine.”</b>
</i><br><br>OMG…This is one of the most interesting stories I have ever read! These three books are amazing. Every single one of them! I am so glad I started this series…turns out they became one of my absolute favorite. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415122ra/819278.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So…Syn is presented as a gift to the Horde King. And as you know…Ryder always delivers! <br><br>The best thing about the book is that we finally get some closure. We learn who (what) Ryder is and all his secrets. We (almost) learn who (what) Syn is. They both will embrace their own destinies and hope at the end they will bring them together. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392802005i/8613707.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I admit…as much as I love Ryder…there were times when he was just pissing me off.   <b>“Woo her,” Ristan continues.<br>“I don’t woo.” <br>“Woo,” he repeats. <br>“I’m not the kind of man to woo anyone. I can make her scream my name to the rafters, isn’t that enough wooing?” <br>“Woo,” Ristan smirks, which only served to irritate me more. <br>“Woo,” I grind out on an exhale.<br>“Yes, woo,” he says, already turning to walk away. I watch his shoulders quake with laughter.<br>“Woo,” I growl. <br>“Woo!” He says over his shaking shoulders. <br>“Fuck me,” I shake my head. <br>“No thanks, not my type…”</b>

I can’t wait to read it!!!!!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392801701i/8613670.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12343778398854827434"><b>4.25 I totally called it stars!</b><br/><br/>This series is clearing addicting. I’ve read the first three books back to back and I’m getting ready to read the next book.<br/><br/>The thing that I enjoy most about this series is that the characters progress and change for the BETTER with each book.   <span id="freeText12343778398854827434" style="display:none"><b>4.25 I totally called it stars!</b><br /><br />This series is clearing addicting. I’ve read the first three books back to back and I’m getting ready to read the next book.<br /><br />The thing that I enjoy most about this series is that the characters progress and change for the BETTER with each book. I really do love that. I also love that the main storyline is Ryder and Synthia because it is a love tory right?<br /><br />Synthia is in the Horde kingdom and it’s so awesome reading about her in the place and above all, pregnant! Gah, I love a pregnant Heroine. I love how everyone fusses over and I love all the crazy pregnant emotional rants she goes through. It’s cute, adorable and endearing.<br /><br />I love how the side characters become more and I love Synthia’s relationships with the elite guards, I’m looking forward to their books.<br /><br />There’s a lot that goes on with politics, steam and where do Ryder and Syn come to play? Well, everything will be answered and then some. <br /></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer931711630" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3713776640887306822"><b>WOW ...</b><br/><br/>I'm trying to think of what I can say. <br/><br/>I'm just ...<br/><br/>**takes deep breaths** <br/><br/>I've been reading this series for a couple days. I have lived and breathed these characters. I couldn't do <b>ANYTHING</b> but read once I started. <br/><br/>Moving was painful. <br/>Having to attend to life was just not doable. <br/><br/><b>I became addicted.</b> <br/><br/>I was completely <b>CONSUMED,</b> taken in every sense of the word. I literately walked around with some sort of reading device in my hands for <b>THREE DAYS.</b> One was always being charged. I rotated them</span>
  <span id="freeText3713776640887306822" style="display:none"><b>WOW ...</b><br /><br />I'm trying to think of what I can say. <br /><br />I'm just ...<br /><br />**takes deep breaths** <br /><br />I've been reading this series for a couple days. I have lived and breathed these characters. I couldn't do <b>ANYTHING</b> but read once I started. <br /><br />Moving was painful. <br />Having to attend to life was just not doable. <br /><br /><b>I became addicted.</b> <br /><br />I was completely <b>CONSUMED,</b> taken in every sense of the word. I literately walked around with some sort of reading device in my hands for <b>THREE DAYS.</b> One was always being charged. I rotated them. When I laid my head down at night I dreamt of these books, this world the author created. The first thought on my mind when I awoke was Ry, Syn, Ristan, Z, Adam and the cast of The Fae Chronicles. <br /><br />This story was compelling, all consuming, magical, erotic and brilliant. <br /><br />I'm hungover, still living in my Kindle with these <b>SOUL SHATTERING</b> characters. <br /><br />I haven't felt this OWNED by a PNR series in a LONG time. I wish I could <b>EXPRESS</b> myself right now in a way that would make you run and buy these books. <br /><br />I'm just... Shit, I'm emotionally exhausted, mentally drained, and physically shot, but craving more so bad. <br /><br /><b>THESE BOOKS ARE A DRUG!</b> <br /><br />A strong, brilliant drug, crafted so perfectly that every word had my heart strumming for more. The magic in the writing was breathtaking. The personality of the characters heartwarming.<br /><br /><b>IT'S EVERYTHING A SERIES SHOULD BE!</b><br /><br />I can't wait for book 4! <br /><br /><b>THIS IS ONE OF THE BEST PNR SERIES I HAVE EVER READ.</b> I'll never forget it. <br /><br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer881367193" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12695211290076541110"><b>
  <i>“You have to trust what you are, and what you want the most, to find who you truly are.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Wow! <br/><br/>I admit, I have a bit of a love-hate relationship with this series. Aspects of the previous books have annoyed me, and I have a few issues with the writing, but the story is just so damn addictive! And things take a huge twist in this book, and it all starts to become just a little bit awesome!<br/><br/>This book picks up immediately after the ending of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17980013.Taunting_Destiny__The_Fae_Chronicles__2_' title='Taunting Destiny (The Fae Chronicles #2) by Amelia Hutchins' rel='nofollow noopener'>Taunting Destiny</a>, continuing to build the tension from wh</span>
  <span id="freeText12695211290076541110" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“You have to trust what you are, and what you want the most, to find who you truly are.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Wow! <br /><br />I admit, I have a bit of a love-hate relationship with this series. Aspects of the previous books have annoyed me, and I have a few issues with the writing, but the story is just so damn addictive! And things take a huge twist in this book, and it all starts to become just a little bit awesome!<br /><br />This book picks up immediately after the ending of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17980013.Taunting_Destiny__The_Fae_Chronicles__2_" title="Taunting Destiny (The Fae Chronicles #2) by Amelia Hutchins" rel="nofollow noopener">Taunting Destiny</a>, continuing to build the tension from where the story left off, but the resolution of the cliffy comes pretty early on. I’m happy to say that even though I picked the big bombshell, it didn’t diminish the excitement of the moment for me, and from that moment on, I was sucked right in.<br /><br />With brand new insight into who she is, Synthia is thrust into yet another new world, and quickly sets about finding her place. She encounters obstacles along the way, but starts to accept her new life, and comes to realise exactly what it is that she wants, and then stands strong while fighting hard to claim it. <br /><br />Oh yes, the feels are getting more intense as Syn and Ryder falls even harder for each other. And we’re finally starting to get some swoony stuff!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“One way or another, I’d have come for you. Fate pushed us together, but destiny knew we belonged together. Now you just have to accept it” </i>
</blockquote><br />As they come to understand their importance to each other, Syn and Ryder finally start to open up to each other, and as a result their relationship becomes more functional. Even big, badass Ryder starts to show his emotional side! We got to see the beginnings of the depth of his feelings for Syn in the last book, and I loved getting to see more of that as he realises exactly what she means to him and acknowledges that – both to himself and to others. I loved it!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She’s my fucking anchor, and no one will take her from me again, not even to save this world.”<br /><br />“She’s mine, all mine. She’s my little freak in bed. My submissive to my inner control freak. She comes out of that perfect little shell and becomes my everything. My world.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Ryder is such a badass! And his dominance and need for control translates over to the bedroom, and HOT. DAMN!!! There is sooooo much sex in this book! It’s full on, it’s explicit, it’s a little bit nasty and it’s hot as hell! Ryder has some incredible moves – and when you throw his magic into the mix it all of a sudden seems very unfair to be human. He also has a wickedly filthy mouth, and likes to keep things dirty. And way to go Syn, for keeping up with him!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Bend me over, pull my hair, whisper more dirty things that will make me tremble with need, Ryder, and then fuck me like you mean it. Fuck me like I am the air you need to live. I don’t want to be your world; I just want to be your favorite part of it.”</i>
</blockquote><br />And oh yeah, can he deliver!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You like me buried deep inside your sweet flesh?” <br />Another yes is screamed from her lips. <br />“Then come for me. Show me how much you like it. Come fast and hard, so I can fuck your sweet flesh harder.” I release her hands and hair, and watch as she crumbles to the bed. Fuck, she’s a goddess!</i>
</blockquote><br />Phew! *fans self*<br /><br />I also need to take a moment to celebrate the awesome that is Ristan. I freakin’ love that demon! Crude, sarcastic, and dirty, he is absolutely hilarious, but also has a heart of gold. He is a big part of this book, and I loved every moment with him - particularly his bantering with both Ryder and Syn.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Here,” he said, handing me one of several short swords from beneath his cloak. “Now just because I’m letting you touch my sword and play with it, Flower, doesn’t mean we’re dating and shit. Don’t go getting the wrong impression here. I like my balls. Ryder would be having them for dinner if he thought there was something going on between us. Now, I know the lure of a Demon is strong, but this shit between us? It’s platonic. I like you, and even though the allure of swapping spit between us is appealing, fight it.” <br />“Seriously, Demon, you’re so full of it,” I said, shaking my head as he grinned from ear to ear. <br />“C’mon, admit it. You like me,” he said…<br />“Oh I like you, but I like you better from a safe distance,” I replied with a wide grin. <br />“Come on, admit it, you want me.” <br />“Dream on, Demon.” </i>
</blockquote><br />The romance is definitely more of a focus in this book, but with battles, riddles, plots and scheming, once again this book is full on from start to finish. And OMG, there are some massive reveals! Right when you think you finally understand what is going on, yet another bomb gets dropped, leading up to the epic game changer right at the end. It’s going to have big implications for the rest of the series, and I’m looking forward to seeing how it all plays out.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this one. 4 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12695211290076541110" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

He said to look for him but where is he? <br/><br/>I'm still really enjoying Syn and Ryder. Every time I get frustrated by Syn, especially when she gets whiny, I just try to remember how young she is and everything she's gone through. Ryder can be infuriating too especially with some of the things he says to Syn. But then we get his POV and I love hearing what all he feels for Syn.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400785833i/9721492.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Believe it or</span>

The Beast part was bordering on a bit weird but it still worked. <br><br>There are more intense and emotional scenes in this book with what's happening with Syn and the contract for Ryder. Plus we get to learn a lot more about Syn and when she finally comes into her powers. The scene with Ristan was a bit tough. <br><br>I really liked that we are finally getting some answers and that things are coming together.     <a title="Lia Angelidou" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7348023-lia-angelidou"><img alt="Lia Angelidou" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506709257p2/7348023.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1203689628?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7348023-lia-angelidou?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7348023-lia-angelidou?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7348023-lia-angelidou?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7348023-lia-angelidou?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7348023-lia-angelidou?shelf=pretty-cover">pretty-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7348023-lia-angelidou?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1203689628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer849724648689727651"> <b>"I still have choices. Embracing what destiny has planned for me, or escaping it!"</b><br/><br/> I was sure that the third book would be the best book. <i> 4.5 stars this time!</i><br/>The plot was as expected mindblowing and the characters grew on me even more. I feel like I am already having a book hangover. I can't take the world that Mrs. Hutchins created out of my mind; I even dreamt about it last night because I was so into the book. <br/> She is great at describing emotions and feelings and of course the amazing scene</span>
  <span id="freeText849724648689727651" style="display:none"> <b>"I still have choices. Embracing what destiny has planned for me, or escaping it!"</b><br /><br /> I was sure that the third book would be the best book. <i> 4.5 stars this time!</i><br />The plot was as expected mindblowing and the characters grew on me even more. I feel like I am already having a book hangover. I can't take the world that Mrs. Hutchins created out of my mind; I even dreamt about it last night because I was so into the book. <br /> She is great at describing emotions and feelings and of course the amazing scenery that Faery was supposed to have. I wish I could live there, visiting all these amazing places. In book three we got to know more about Faery and about Fae traditions and behavior the bad way just like poor Syn did. She was through a lot and yet she found the strenght to go against destiny and prove to anyone who doubted her that she is not some weak damsel in distress but an amazing warrior goddess who can protect the people she loves.<br /> I am glad that all characters are actually appealing to me, well except the villains of course. I hate reading books with characters I dislike because it makes finishing the book difficult to me. Ryder kind of annoyed me at first but thank god he changed for his own good. Ristan is still the same amazing, hot, smartass demon I love and I need to know more about him!<br /> Anyway other than that, the sex was steamy, the annoying repeat of thoughts stopped and I don't think there's anything left that would bother me now. Off to read book number four.</span>
  <a data-text-id="849724648689727651" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2+JBgv7ft2cCimeaBBw4cZyo5UTX56H3baWpUJoSgeQrXxXaDVxGKH6QfUpMW19/kW5ph8IOAVwY9ogUBnG9AQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OgQc1GNwVLA92zoUGfHRcQltUTFAPiMl4fSIJqBDgAvKuUiMkPOl/0HBIMRRtrZ/BKvd8lXXg46Up6liPCC87g==')})
  }

But the nightmare isn’t over. Callie wears the physical reminders of her time as a captive, and mounting evidence suggests the Thief of Souls is still out there.\n \nWhen a fae celebration thrusts Callie and her mate, Desmond Flynn, into the Kingdom of Flora, they take their investigation with them. But under the bright lights and striking blooms of the realm, they find there are more immediate issues to deal with. No place is more uniquely savage than the great fae halls, and no amount of bargains can save Callie from royal intrigues.\n \nFairies play dangerous games. Some want love, some want vengeance, some want flesh, and some want things too unspeakable to utter. One thing is for sure: no one is who they appear to be. Not even Des, who only grows more enigmatic with every passing secret.\n \nBut the Kingdom of Flora has its own secrets, from bleeding trees to branded slaves and missing guards.
